      <article id="post-575" class="post post-575 type-post status-publish format-standard has-post-thumbnail hentry category-uncategorized category-development-en tag-async tag-azure tag-gzip tag-jquery tag-nodejs tag-webjobs"> 
       <div class="fusion-flexslider flexslider fusion-flexslider-loading post-slideshow fusion-post-slideshow"> 
        <ul class="slides"> 
         <li> <a href="http://medienstudio.net/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/scraping-websites-json-azure-webjobs-nodejs-jquery-asyncjs-gzip-medienstudio.net_.jpg" data-rel="iLightbox[gallery575]" title="" data-title="scraping-websites-json-azure-webjobs-nodejs-jquery-asyncjs-gzip-medienstudio.net" data-caption=""> <span class="screen-reader-text">View Larger Image</span> <img width="1000" height="600" src="http://medienstudio.net/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/scraping-websites-json-azure-webjobs-nodejs-jquery-asyncjs-gzip-medienstudio.net_-800x480.jpg" class="attachment-full size-full wp-post-image" alt="" srcset="http://medienstudio.net/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/scraping-websites-json-azure-webjobs-nodejs-jquery-asyncjs-gzip-medienstudio.net_-200x120.jpg 200w, http://medienstudio.net/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/scraping-websites-json-azure-webjobs-nodejs-jquery-asyncjs-gzip-medienstudio.net_-400x240.jpg 400w, http://medienstudio.net/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/scraping-websites-json-azure-webjobs-nodejs-jquery-asyncjs-gzip-medienstudio.net_-600x360.jpg 600w, http://medienstudio.net/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/scraping-websites-json-azure-webjobs-nodejs-jquery-asyncjs-gzip-medienstudio.net_-800x480.jpg 800w, http://medienstudio.net/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/scraping-websites-json-azure-webjobs-nodejs-jquery-asyncjs-gzip-medienstudio.net_.jpg 1000w" sizes="(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 767px"> </a> </li> 
        </ul> 
       </div> 
       <h2 class="entry-title fusion-post-title">Scraping Websites using Azure WebJobs, Node.js, jQuery, Async.js &amp; gizp</h2> 
       <div class="post-content"> 
        <p>In this post we’ll look at scraping Websites on a regular basis using Azure WebJobs &amp; Node.js (jQuery&nbsp;/ cheerio) and returning the data as JSON.</p> 
        <p>In the example below we’ll each week grab the&nbsp;apps that are&nbsp;on sale as part of the “Red Stripe Deals” in the Windows Store. The resulting&nbsp;app details will be put into a JSON file that can be consumed for example by a mobile app.</p> 
        <p><span id="more-575"></span></p> 
        <h2>Crawling &amp; Scraping: be responsible</h2> 
        <p>There’s already enough content out there about the ethics of scraping data from the web, so I won’t get into that at this point. However, we really do not want to break the site we try to get the data from. Especially when using powerful tools like Azure we should make sure not to DOS the server.</p> 
        <p>That’s why we’re using tools like <a onclick="javascript:pageTracker._trackPageview('/outgoing/github.com/caolan/async');" href="https://github.com/caolan/async">Async.js</a>&nbsp;and the zlib Library (which is part of Node.js) to limit bandwidth usage.</p> 
        <h2>Tools</h2> 
        <ul> 
         <li><a onclick="javascript:pageTracker._trackPageview('/outgoing/azure.microsoft.com/en-us/');" href="https://azure.microsoft.com/en-us/">Windows Azure Account</a></li> 
         <li><a onclick="javascript:pageTracker._trackPageview('/outgoing/nodejs.org/en/');" href="https://nodejs.org/en/">NodeJS</a></li> 
         <li><a onclick="javascript:pageTracker._trackPageview('/outgoing/www.microsoft.com/web/webmatrix/');" href="https://www.microsoft.com/web/webmatrix/">Microsoft Webmatrix</a></li> 
        </ul> 
        <h2>First things first</h2> 
        <p>To create a new WebJob we first need an Azure Web App for it to run in. The free F1 tier will do just fine, especially for testing purposes.</p> 
        <p><img class="alignnone size-full wp-image-545" src="http://medienstudio.net/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/azure-new-web-app.jpg" alt="azure new web app" width="888" height="697" srcset="http://medienstudio.net/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/azure-new-web-app-200x157.jpg 200w, http://medienstudio.net/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/azure-new-web-app-300x235.jpg 300w, http://medienstudio.net/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/azure-new-web-app-400x314.jpg 400w, http://medienstudio.net/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/azure-new-web-app-600x471.jpg 600w, http://medienstudio.net/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/azure-new-web-app-768x603.jpg 768w, http://medienstudio.net/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/azure-new-web-app-800x628.jpg 800w, http://medienstudio.net/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/azure-new-web-app.jpg 888w" sizes="(max-width: 888px) 100vw, 888px"></p> 
        <h2>Create a Node.js project</h2> 
        <p>To create a new project we’ll create an empty folder that will eventually contain all the necessary files and which we’ll be able to upload as a .zip-Archive to Azure later on.</p> 
        <p>Inside the new folder open the command prompt (Shift + right click inside the folder) and install the required Node.js packages through npm.</p>
        <!-- Crayon Syntax Highlighter v_2.7.2_beta --> 
        <div id="crayon-59d970db02f8d988924741" class="crayon-syntax crayon-theme-classic crayon-font-monaco crayon-os-pc print-yes notranslate" data-settings=" minimize scroll-mouseover" style=" margin-top: 12px; margin-bottom: 12px; font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;"> 
         <div class="crayon-toolbar" data-settings=" mouseover overlay hide delay" style="font-size: 12px !important;height: 18px !important; line-height: 18px !important;">
          <span class="crayon-title"></span> 
          <div class="crayon-tools" style="font-size: 12px !important;height: 18px !important; line-height: 18px !important;">
           <div class="crayon-button crayon-nums-button" title="Zeilennummern">
            <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
           </div>
           <div class="crayon-button crayon-plain-button" title="Unformatierte Code-Ansicht">
            <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
           </div>
           <div class="crayon-button crayon-wrap-button" title="Zeilenumbruch umschalten">
            <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
           </div>
           <div class="crayon-button crayon-expand-button" title="Code aufklappen">
            <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
           </div>
           <div class="crayon-button crayon-copy-button" title="Copy">
            <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
           </div>

            <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>

         <div class="crayon-info" style="min-height: 16.8px !important; line-height: 16.8px !important;"></div> 
         <div class="crayon-plain-wrap">
          <textarea wrap="soft" class="crayon-plain print-no" data-settings="dblclick" readonly style="-moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4; font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;">
npm install request</textarea>
         </div> 
         <div class="crayon-main" style=""> 
          <table class="crayon-table"> 
           <tbody>
            <tr class="crayon-row">

        <p> <a onclick="javascript:pageTracker._trackPageview('/outgoing/github.com/caolan/async');" href="https://github.com/caolan/async">async</a> will help us to throttle requests by using it’s queue function.</p> 
        <p>Additionally we’ll make use of the following two packages, which are already part of Node.js:</p> 
        <p><a onclick="javascript:pageTracker._trackPageview('/outgoing/github.com/caolan/async');" href="https://github.com/caolan/async">zlib</a>&nbsp;lets us download and extract Websites&nbsp;using gzip which dramatically reduces the overall amount of data transferred.<br> Using <a onclick="javascript:pageTracker._trackPageview('/outgoing/www.tutorialspoint.com/nodejs/nodejs_file_system.htm');" href="http://www.tutorialspoint.com/nodejs/nodejs_file_system.htm">fs</a>&nbsp;we can eventually save our data as a .json-Document to the hard drive.</p>

        <!-- [Format Time: 0.0026 seconds] --> 
        <p> <em>dealsUri</em> our entry page that contains links to all the apps we want to get.<br> <em>baseUri</em> is required for calling the absolute path to the app details pages.<br> <em>outputFilename</em> sets the location for our JSON output.&nbsp;The location varies depending on whether we test locally or if the Script is running inside an Azure WebJob since it’ll <a onclick="javascript:pageTracker._trackPageview('/outgoing/stackoverflow.com/questions/21769095/uri-of-azure-web-jobs-output-file-with-node-js');" href="http://stackoverflow.com/questions/21769095/uri-of-azure-web-jobs-output-file-with-node-js">be copied into a temporary directory</a> before being executed.</p> 
        <h2>The Crawler</h2> 
        <p>We want our script to do the following steps:</p> 
        <ol> 
         <li>Get the main Red-Stripe-Deals page with all the links to the individual apps using gzip:
          <!-- Crayon Syntax Highlighter v_2.7.2_beta --> 
          <div id="crayon-59d970db02faa870715748" class="crayon-syntax crayon-theme-classic crayon-font-monaco crayon-os-pc print-yes notranslate" data-settings=" minimize scroll-mouseover" style=" margin-top: 12px; margin-bottom: 12px; font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;"> 
           <div class="crayon-toolbar" data-settings=" mouseover overlay hide delay" style="font-size: 12px !important;height: 18px !important; line-height: 18px !important;">
            <span class="crayon-title">Loading and de-zipping Deals-Page</span> 
            <div class="crayon-tools" style="font-size: 12px !important;height: 18px !important; line-height: 18px !important;">
             <div class="crayon-button crayon-nums-button" title="Zeilennummern">
              <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
             </div>
             <div class="crayon-button crayon-plain-button" title="Unformatierte Code-Ansicht">
              <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>

             <div class="crayon-button crayon-wrap-button" title="Zeilenumbruch umschalten">
              <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>

             <div class="crayon-button crayon-expand-button" title="Code aufklappen">
              <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>

             <div class="crayon-button crayon-copy-button" title="Copy">
              <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>

              <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
             </div>
             <span class="crayon-language">JavaScript</span>
            </div>
           </div> 
           <div class="crayon-info" style="min-height: 16.8px !important; line-height: 16.8px !important;"></div> 
           <div class="crayon-plain-wrap">
            <textarea wrap="soft" class="crayon-plain print-no" data-settings="dblclick" readonly style="-moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4; font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;">
var loadDeals = function () {
    var options = { 
        url: dealsUri,
        port: 443,
        headers: {
            'User-Agent': 'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 6.3; Trident/7.0; rv:11.0) like Gecko',
            'Accept-Language': 'en-us',
            'Content-Language': 'en-us',
			'Accept-Encoding': 'gzip'
        },
        timeout: 0,
        encoding: null
    };
    request(options, function (err, resp, body) {
        if (err) {
            console.log("error loading page");
        } 
        if (!err) {
            if (resp.headers['content-encoding'] == 'gzip') {
                zlib.gunzip(body, function (err, dezipped) {
                    redstripedealsParser(dezipped.toString());
                });
            } else {
                redstripedealsParser(body);
            }
        }
    });
}</textarea>

         <li>Process the queue one by one getting the app details pages and handing them to our parser.<br> We can choose how many tasks should run at the same time by changing the last parameter in async.queue() – 1 in this case:
          <!-- Crayon Syntax Highlighter v_2.7.2_beta --> 
          <div id="crayon-59d970db02fb2661453063" class="crayon-syntax crayon-theme-classic crayon-font-monaco crayon-os-pc print-yes notranslate" data-settings=" minimize scroll-mouseover" style=" margin-top: 12px; margin-bottom: 12px; font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;"> 
           <div class="crayon-toolbar" data-settings=" mouseover overlay hide delay" style="font-size: 12px !important;height: 18px !important; line-height: 18px !important;">
            <span class="crayon-title">Downloading and de-zipping the app details pages</span> 
            <div class="crayon-tools" style="font-size: 12px !important;height: 18px !important; line-height: 18px !important;">
             <div class="crayon-button crayon-nums-button" title="Zeilennummern">
              <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
             </div>
             <div class="crayon-button crayon-plain-button" title="Unformatierte Code-Ansicht">
              <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
             </div>
             <div class="crayon-button crayon-wrap-button" title="Zeilenumbruch umschalten">
              <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
             </div>
             <div class="crayon-button crayon-expand-button" title="Code aufklappen">
              <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
             </div>
             <div class="crayon-button crayon-copy-button" title="Copy">
              <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
             </div>
             <div class="crayon-button crayon-popup-button" title="Code in einem neuen Fenster anzeigen">
              <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
             </div>
             <span class="crayon-language">JavaScript</span>
            </div>
           </div> 
           <div class="crayon-info" style="min-height: 16.8px !important; line-height: 16.8px !important;"></div> 
           <div class="crayon-plain-wrap">
            <textarea wrap="soft" class="crayon-plain print-no" data-settings="dblclick" readonly style="-moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4; font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;">
var qDetails = async.queue(function (task, callback) {
    console.log("get details: " + task);
	var options = {
		url: task,
		headers: {
			'User-Agent': 'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 6.3; Trident/7.0; rv:11.0) like Gecko',
			'Accept-Language': 'en-us',
			'Content-Language': 'en-us',
			'Accept-Encoding': 'gzip'
		},
		timeout: 0,
        encoding: null
	};
	request(options, function (err, resp, body) {
        if (err)
        {
            console.log("error: " + task);
            throw err;
        }
		if(resp.headers['content-encoding'] == 'gzip'){
			zlib.gunzip(body, function(err, dezipped) {
				GetDetails(dezipped.toString(), task, callback);
			});
		} else {
			GetDetails(body, task, callback);
		}
	}); 
}, 1);</textarea>

          <!-- [Format Time: 0.0047 seconds] --> </li> 
         <li>Extract all relevant app details, again using cheerio. We then push the app into the <em>output </em>array.<br> Don’t forget the callback() telling the async-queue to proceed:
          <!-- Crayon Syntax Highlighter v_2.7.2_beta --> 
          <div id="crayon-59d970db02fb9412712132" class="crayon-syntax crayon-theme-classic crayon-font-monaco crayon-os-pc print-yes notranslate" data-settings=" minimize scroll-mouseover" style=" margin-top: 12px; margin-bottom: 12px; font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;"> 
           <div class="crayon-toolbar" data-settings=" mouseover overlay hide delay" style="font-size: 12px !important;height: 18px !important; line-height: 18px !important;">
            <span class="crayon-title">Extract app details using cheerio</span> 
            <div class="crayon-tools" style="font-size: 12px !important;height: 18px !important; line-height: 18px !important;">
             <div class="crayon-button crayon-nums-button" title="Zeilennummern">
              <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
             </div>
             <div class="crayon-button crayon-plain-button" title="Unformatierte Code-Ansicht">
              <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
             </div>
             <div class="crayon-button crayon-wrap-button" title="Zeilenumbruch umschalten">
              <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
             </div>
             <div class="crayon-button crayon-expand-button" title="Code aufklappen">
              <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
             </div>
             <div class="crayon-button crayon-copy-button" title="Copy">
              <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
             </div>
             <div class="crayon-button crayon-popup-button" title="Code in einem neuen Fenster anzeigen">
              <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
             </div>
             <span class="crayon-language">JavaScript</span>
            </div>
           </div> 
           <div class="crayon-info" style="min-height: 16.8px !important; line-height: 16.8px !important;"></div> 
           <div class="crayon-plain-wrap">
            <textarea wrap="soft" class="crayon-plain print-no" data-settings="dblclick" readonly style="-moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4; font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;">
var GetDetails = function (body, task, callback) {
    console.log("parse details: " + task);
    $ = cheerio.load(body);

    var app = {};
    
    app["title"] = $('#page-title').text();
    app["image"] = "http:" + $('.ph-logo &gt; img').first().attr('src').toString();
    app["description"] = $('.showmore  &gt; p').first().text();
    app["price"] = $('.srv_price &gt; span').first().text();
    app["ratingValue"] = $('.srv_ratingsScore.win-rating-average').first().text();
    app["ratingCount"] = $('.win-rating-total').first().text().replace(/\D/g, '');
    app["packageSize"] = $('.metadata-list-content &gt; div').eq(2).text().replace("\r\n", "").trim();
    app["publisher"] = $('.metadata-list-content &gt; div').eq(0).text().replace("\r\n", "").trim();

    output.push(app);
    callback();
}</textarea>

qDetails.drain = function ()
{
	fs.writeFile(outputFilename, JSON.stringify(output, null), function (err)
	{
		if (err)
		{
			console.log(err);
		} else
		{
			console.log("JSON saved to " + outputFilename);
		}
	});
}</textarea>

          <!-- [Format Time: 0.0002 seconds] --> </li> 
        </ol> 
        <p>You can&nbsp;find the complete code also as a&nbsp;<a onclick="javascript:pageTracker._trackPageview('/outgoing/gist.github.com/ThomasPe/a6df2e4135ba1815b30c49a9495755f0');" href="https://gist.github.com/ThomasPe/a6df2e4135ba1815b30c49a9495755f0">Github Gist</a>.<br> <script src="https://gist.github.com/ThomasPe/a6df2e4135ba1815b30c49a9495755f0.js"></script><br> Now we can test the script from the command line:</p>
        <!-- Crayon Syntax Highlighter v_2.7.2_beta --> 
        <div id="crayon-59d970db02fc5224434097" class="crayon-syntax crayon-theme-classic crayon-font-monaco crayon-os-pc print-yes notranslate" data-settings=" minimize scroll-mouseover" style=" margin-top: 12px; margin-bottom: 12px; font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;"> 
         <div class="crayon-toolbar" data-settings=" mouseover overlay hide delay" style="font-size: 12px !important;height: 18px !important; line-height: 18px !important;">
          <span class="crayon-title"></span> 
          <div class="crayon-tools" style="font-size: 12px !important;height: 18px !important; line-height: 18px !important;">
           <div class="crayon-button crayon-nums-button" title="Zeilennummern">
            <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
           </div>
           <div class="crayon-button crayon-plain-button" title="Unformatierte Code-Ansicht">

         </div> 
         <div class="crayon-info" style="min-height: 16.8px !important; line-height: 16.8px !important;"></div> 
         <div class="crayon-plain-wrap">
          <textarea wrap="soft" class="crayon-plain print-no" data-settings="dblclick" readonly style="-moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4; font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;">
node app.js</textarea>
         </div> 
         <div class="crayon-main" style=""> 
          <table class="crayon-table"> 
           <tbody>
            <tr class="crayon-row"> 
             <td class="crayon-nums " data-settings="show">

                1
               </div>
              </div> </td> 
             <td class="crayon-code">
              <div class="crayon-pre" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;">
               <div class="crayon-line" id="crayon-59d970db02fc5224434097-1">
                <span class="crayon-e">node </span>
                <span class="crayon-v">app</span>
                <span class="crayon-sy">.</span>
                <span class="crayon-v">js</span>
               </div>
              </div></td> 
            </tr> 
           </tbody>
          </table> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <!-- [Format Time: 0.0002 seconds] --> 
        <p> </p>
        <h2>Scheduling the WebJob</h2> 
        <p>After successfully running the script locally we change the output location for Azure and afterwards compress the whole folder into a regular&nbsp;.zip file.</p> 
        <p>In order to create a WebJob that actually runs on a schedule we need to sign into the <a onclick="javascript:pageTracker._trackPageview('/outgoing/manage.windowsazure.com');" href="https://manage.windowsazure.com">old Azure portal</a>. There it’s possible to create a new WebJob inside our previously created web app. Just enter a new name, upload the zip file and select a region that you want the job to run in.</p> 
        <p><img class="alignnone size-full wp-image-563" src="http://medienstudio.net/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/webjobs-schedule-medienstudio.net_..jpg" alt="webjobs-schedule-medienstudio.net." width="1414" height="817" srcset="http://medienstudio.net/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/webjobs-schedule-medienstudio.net_.-200x116.jpg 200w, http://medienstudio.net/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/webjobs-schedule-medienstudio.net_.-300x173.jpg 300w, http://medienstudio.net/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/webjobs-schedule-medienstudio.net_.-400x231.jpg 400w, http://medienstudio.net/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/webjobs-schedule-medienstudio.net_.-600x347.jpg 600w, http://medienstudio.net/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/webjobs-schedule-medienstudio.net_.-768x444.jpg 768w, http://medienstudio.net/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/webjobs-schedule-medienstudio.net_.-800x462.jpg 800w, http://medienstudio.net/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/webjobs-schedule-medienstudio.net_.-1024x592.jpg 1024w, http://medienstudio.net/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/webjobs-schedule-medienstudio.net_.-1200x693.jpg 1200w, http://medienstudio.net/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/webjobs-schedule-medienstudio.net_..jpg 1414w" sizes="(max-width: 1414px) 100vw, 1414px"><br> For the second step we choose when the script should be executed. In our case it’s sufficient to run the Job just once a week as the deals won’t change more often than that.</p> 
        <p><img class="alignnone size-full wp-image-562" src="http://medienstudio.net/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/webjobs-schedule-2-medienstudio.net_.jpg" alt="webjobs-schedule-2-medienstudio.net" width="1414" height="817" srcset="http://medienstudio.net/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/webjobs-schedule-2-medienstudio.net_-200x116.jpg 200w, http://medienstudio.net/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/webjobs-schedule-2-medienstudio.net_-300x173.jpg 300w, http://medienstudio.net/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/webjobs-schedule-2-medienstudio.net_-400x231.jpg 400w, http://medienstudio.net/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/webjobs-schedule-2-medienstudio.net_-600x347.jpg 600w, http://medienstudio.net/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/webjobs-schedule-2-medienstudio.net_-768x444.jpg 768w, http://medienstudio.net/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/webjobs-schedule-2-medienstudio.net_-800x462.jpg 800w, http://medienstudio.net/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/webjobs-schedule-2-medienstudio.net_-1024x592.jpg 1024w, http://medienstudio.net/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/webjobs-schedule-2-medienstudio.net_-1200x693.jpg 1200w, http://medienstudio.net/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/webjobs-schedule-2-medienstudio.net_.jpg 1414w" sizes="(max-width: 1414px) 100vw, 1414px"></p> 
        <p>As soon as the job is created we can try running it for the first time. If we’ve done everything right we should then get a “Success” in the results column.</p> 
        <h2>Editing a WebJob Script</h2> 
        <p>It is actually fairly easy to edit an active WebJob script (which we would never do in a productive environment!). Using Microsoft Webmatrix makes it really easy to sign into your Microsoft / Azure account and just remotely edit your web apps.</p> 
        <p><img class="alignnone size-full wp-image-569" src="http://medienstudio.net/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/webmatrix-webjobs-medienstudio.net_.jpg" alt="webmatrix-webjobs-medienstudio.net" width="1250" height="847" srcset="http://medienstudio.net/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/webmatrix-webjobs-medienstudio.net_-200x136.jpg 200w, http://medienstudio.net/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/webmatrix-webjobs-medienstudio.net_-300x203.jpg 300w, http://medienstudio.net/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/webmatrix-webjobs-medienstudio.net_-400x271.jpg 400w, http://medienstudio.net/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/webmatrix-webjobs-medienstudio.net_-600x407.jpg 600w, http://medienstudio.net/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/webmatrix-webjobs-medienstudio.net_-768x520.jpg 768w, http://medienstudio.net/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/webmatrix-webjobs-medienstudio.net_-800x542.jpg 800w, http://medienstudio.net/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/webmatrix-webjobs-medienstudio.net_-1024x694.jpg 1024w, http://medienstudio.net/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/webmatrix-webjobs-medienstudio.net_-1200x813.jpg 1200w, http://medienstudio.net/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/webmatrix-webjobs-medienstudio.net_.jpg 1250w" sizes="(max-width: 1250px) 100vw, 1250px"></p> 
        <h2>Retrieving the JSON result</h2> 
        <p>Finally we want to consume our JSON document for example inside a mobile app. However, there’s a tiny issue: Azure Websites won’t serve any static JSON by default. This can be fixed by placing the following code inside the Web.config inside the root folder of the server:</p>
        <!-- Crayon Syntax Highlighter v_2.7.2_beta --> 
        <div id="crayon-59d970db02fc9419380153" class="crayon-syntax crayon-theme-classic crayon-font-monaco crayon-os-pc print-yes notranslate" data-settings=" minimize scroll-mouseover" style=" margin-top: 12px; margin-bottom: 12px; font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;"> 
         <div class="crayon-toolbar" data-settings=" mouseover overlay hide delay" style="font-size: 12px !important;height: 18px !important; line-height: 18px !important;">
          <span class="crayon-title"></span> 
          <div class="crayon-tools" style="font-size: 12px !important;height: 18px !important; line-height: 18px !important;">
           <span class="crayon-mixed-highlight" title="Enthält verschiedene Sprachen"></span>
           <div class="crayon-button crayon-nums-button" title="Zeilennummern">
            <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
           </div>
           <div class="crayon-button crayon-plain-button" title="Unformatierte Code-Ansicht">
            <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
           </div>
           <div class="crayon-button crayon-wrap-button" title="Zeilenumbruch umschalten">
            <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
           </div>
           <div class="crayon-button crayon-expand-button" title="Code aufklappen">
            <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
           </div>
           <div class="crayon-button crayon-copy-button" title="Copy">
            <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
           </div>
           <div class="crayon-button crayon-popup-button" title="Code in einem neuen Fenster anzeigen">
            <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
           </div>
          </div>
         </div> 
         <div class="crayon-info" style="min-height: 16.8px !important; line-height: 16.8px !important;"></div> 
         <div class="crayon-plain-wrap">
          <textarea wrap="soft" class="crayon-plain print-no" data-settings="dblclick" readonly style="-moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4; font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;">
&lt;?xml version="1.0"?&gt;
 
&lt;configuration&gt;
    &lt;system.webServer&gt;
        &lt;staticContent&gt;
            &lt;mimeMap fileExtension=".json" mimeType="application/json" /&gt;
     &lt;/staticContent&gt;
    &lt;/system.webServer&gt;
&lt;/configuration&gt;</textarea>
         </div>

						tellFrameNewParent();

						return returnValue;
					};
